class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-mw-body-content” id=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-mw-content-text” lang=”en”> <div class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-mw-parser-output”> <div class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-thumbinner”> <div class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-thumbcaption”> <div class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-magnify”> </div> <span style=”font-size: xx-small;”> K’awiil effigy cast from&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tikal” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank” title=”Tikal”>Tikal</a></span></div> </div> </div> <span style=”font-size: xx-small;”><strong>K’awiil</strong>, in the Post-Classic codices corresponding to&nbsp;<strong>God K</strong>, is a&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maya_civilization” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank” title=”Maya civilization”>Maya</a>&nbsp;deity identified with lightning, serpents, fertility and maize. He is characterized by a zoomorphic head, with large eyes, long, upturned snout and attenuated serpent tooth.<sup class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-reference” id=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-cite_ref-1”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/K%27awiil#cite_note-1” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank”>[1]</a></sup>&nbsp;A torch, stone celt, or cigar, normally emitting smoke, comes out of his forehead, while a serpent leg represents a lightning bolt. In this way, K’awiil personifies the lightning axe both of the rain deity and of the king as depicted on his stelae.</span><br /> <h2> <span class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-mw-headline” id=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-Narratives_and_scenes”><span style=”font-size: xx-small;”>Narratives and scenes</span></span></h2> <span style=”font-size: xx-small;”>Lightnings play a crucial role in tales dealing with the creation of the world and its preparation for the advent of mankind. In the cosmogony of the Popol Vuh, three Lightning deities identified with the ‘Heart of the Sky’ (among whom&nbsp;<em>Huraqan</em>&nbsp;‘One-Leg’) create the earth out of the primordial sea, and people it with animals. Bolon Dzacab plays an important, if not very clear role in the cosmogonical myth related in the Book of&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chilam_Balam” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank” title=”Chilam Balam”>Chilam Balam</a>&nbsp;of Chumayel, where he is identified with wrapped-up seeds.<sup class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-reference” id=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-cite_ref-4”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/K%27awiil#cite_note-4” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank”>[4]</a></sup>&nbsp;The rain gods or their lightnings once opened up the Maize Mountain, making the maize seeds available to mankind.</span><br /> <h2> <span class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-mw-headline” id=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-Functions”><span style=”font-size: xx-small;”>Functions</span></span></h2> <span style=”font-size: xx-small;”>The illustrated katun cycle of the&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paris_Codex” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank” title=”Paris Codex”>Paris Codex</a>&nbsp;suggests that the presentation of the head of K’awiil – perhaps holding the promise of ‘Innumerable Generations’&nbsp;– was part of the king’s ritual inauguration and accession to the throne. K’awiil not only embodied the king’s war-like lightning power, but also his power to bring agricultural prosperity to his subjects: The Lightning deity was a god of agricultural abundance, and of the maize and cacao seeds in particular. Therefore, he is often depicted with a sack of grains, sometimes accompanied by the expression&nbsp;<em>hun yax(al) hun k’an(al)</em>&nbsp;‘abundance’.<sup class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-reference” id=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-cite_ref-5”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/K%27awiil#cite_note-5” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank”>[5]</a></sup></span></div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div He supposedly lived in the windy mists above the floodwaters and repeatedly invoked “earth” until land came up from the seas.</span></div> <div class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-mw-content-ltr” dir=”ltr” id=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-mw-content-text” lang=”en”> <div class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-mw-parser-output”> <div style=’color: #333333; font-family: “Helvetica Neue Light”,HelveticaNeue-Light,”Helvetica Neue”,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;’> <span style=”font-size: xx-small;”>His name, understood as ‘One-Leg’, suggests&nbsp;<a class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/God_K” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank” title=”God K”>god K</a>&nbsp;of Postclassic and Classic Maya iconography, a deity of lightning with one human leg,<sup class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-reference” id=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-cite_ref-4”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Huracan#cite_note-4” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank”>[4]</a></sup>&nbsp;and one leg shaped like a serpent. God K is commonly referred to as Bolon Tzacab and K’awiil or Kauil. The name may ultimately derive from&nbsp;<em>huracan</em>, a&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carib_language” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank” title=”Carib language”>Carib</a>&nbsp;word,<sup class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-reference” id=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-cite_ref-5”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Huracan#cite_note-5” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank”>[5]</a></sup>&nbsp;and the source of the words&nbsp;<em><a class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hurricane” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank” title=”Hurricane”>hurricane</a></em>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<em><a class=”gmail-m_4257746817933585648gmail-m_-6473932902733423782m_6076646303687409657gmail-m_2525634793871947491gmail-m_8254789373832111845gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Orcan” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank” title=”Orcan”>orcan</a></em>&nbsp;(<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_windstorm” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank” title=”European windstorm”>Eur<wbr></wbr>opean windstorm</a>). Huracan also helped destroy the manikins, the results of their second try. Huracan sent dogs and turkeys into the manikin’s homes proclaiming revenge for the dogs and turkeys slain and eaten. Also, frying pans, mortars, pestles, and even stones came alive. The frying pans complained about their mouths being filled with ash and declared that they will be treated as them. The mortars complained about being banged with a pestle every day and that they will be beaten by pestles as their punishment. The pestles complained about their mouths being filled with grain each and every day. Finally, the stones shot out of the fireplace crushing the helpless manikins. Some sought refuge in trees but fell off after the branches shook them down. Some sought refuge in caves, but huge boulders closed the entrance entombing them forever. Some say you can still hear their sad wails to this day. The survivors ran into the forest and were chased by Huracan and the dogs and turkeys. They ran day and night until they could not go on. Huracan was pleased that there was no more manikins and so he walked until he found a field full of corn. He and Gúcumatz,the plumed serpent, handed the corn to Xmucane, who mixed corn with water to make dough. Out of this dough they made four men, Jaguar Quitze, Jaguar Night, Not Right Now and Dark Jaguar. Humans used to be able to do anything, fly, see oceans from far away, and inside rocks. Huracan clouded their vision so that they couldn’t see so far. Huracan also sent Hunahpu and Xbalanque on their missions and presided over the decapitation of Zipacna the earth monster.</span></div> <div style=’color: #333333; font-family: “Helvetica Neue (TI) is an umbrella term coined by troubled unfortunates and&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Paranoia” title=”Paranoia”>paranoid</a>&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Crank” title=”Crank”>cranks</a>&nbsp;who insist that they are all, individually, on the receiving end of a massive covert harassment conspiracy of highly&nbsp;<s>convoluted</s>&nbsp;malignant intent. As is to be expected (because paranoid delusions respect no borders), TIs are found around the world—from North America and Western Europe<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-3”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-3”>[2]</a></sup><sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-4”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-4”>[3]</a></sup><sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-5”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-5”>[4]</a></sup>&nbsp;to Asia.<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-6”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-6”>[5]</a></sup><br /> The vast majority of TIs consider themselves to be victims of inchoate, ongoing and relentless “touchless torture” plots. The nature of these alleged “attacks” varies among TIs but generally involves some combination of&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Persecution_complex” title=”Persecution complex”>asinine drama</a>&nbsp;with&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Pseudoscience” title=”Pseudoscience”>pseudoscientific</a>&nbsp;flummery and/or improbable, coordinated malicious actions. Their written laments are replete with references to&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/MKULTRA” title=”MKULTRA”>MKULTRA</a>,&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation” title=”Federal Bureau of Investigation”>COINTELPRO</a>, and various government and corporate weapons programs (along with more&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Oxymoron” title=”Oxymoron”>benign military programs</a>&nbsp;unrelated to surveillance, such as&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/HAARP” title=”HAARP”>HAARP</a>). The paranoia was further fed by&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Edward_Snowden” title=”Edward Snowden”>Edward Snowden</a>’s revelations about the global surveillance undertaken by the&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/NSA” title=”NSA”>NSA</a>&nbsp;and its counterparts in allied countries, although some TI’s dismiss Snowden as a “false flag” or “limited hangout” operation given that none of his revealed NSA documents point to the targeting of individuals for touchless torture, gangstalking, and all that jazz.<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-21”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-21”>[18]</a></sup><br /> Concern—even alarm—about the NSA’s global surveillance apparatus and its impact on civil liberties is an entirely rational position. So is outrage over COINTELPRO, and activism to avoid repeat performances from the FBI and other Big Brother agencies. But, to understate, the TI movement is not characterized by such rational interests and justified fears.<br /> As revealed by the Snowden leaks in 2013, only small fraction of Internet users are actually placed under surveillance,<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-boingboing_22-0”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-boingboing-22”>[19]</a></sup>&nbsp;although the productivity of doing so is questionable.<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-23”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-23”>[20]</a></sup>&nbsp;For your boring Joe, their NSA’s database entry is flushed every two or thirty days (because it’s a waste of resources); however, if an individual is under suspicion, then the collected data is held indefinitely. Anyone found searching up Tails or&nbsp;<a class=”gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Tor” title=”Tor”>Tor</a>&nbsp;is added to a list indefinitely to be placed under surveillance.<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-boingboing_22-1”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-boingboing-22”>[19]</a></sup><sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-24”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-24”>[21]</a></sup>&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Nothing_to_hide” title=”Nothing to hide”>This falls under the assumption that these people have something to hide</a>.<br /> <h3> <span class=”gmail-mw-headline” id=”gmail-JTRIG”>JTRIG</span><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection”><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection-bracket”>[</span><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/w/index.php?title=Targeted_Individuals&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4” title=”Edit section: JTRIG”>edit</a><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection-bracket”>]</span></span></h3> Of the many Snowden NSA revelations, none got TIs more excited than&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Glenn_Greenwald” title=”Glenn Greenwald”>Glenn Greenwald</a>’s reporting on the Joint Threat Research Intelligence Group, or JTRIG. This (reprehensible and actually alarming) program undertaken by the British version of the NSA, and in partnership with them, involves;<br /> <blockquote class=”gmail-letter”> Among the core self-identified purposes of JTRIG are two tactics: (1) to inject all sorts of false material onto the internet in order to destroy the reputation of its targets; and (2) to use social sciences and other techniques to manipulate online discourse and activism to generate outcomes it considers desirable. To see how extremist these programs are, just consider the tactics they boast of using to achieve those ends: “false flag operations” (posting material to the internet and falsely attributing it to someone else), fake victim blog posts (pretending to be a victim of the individual whose reputation they want to destroy), and posting “negative information” on various forums.<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-JTRIG_25-0”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-JTRIG-25”>[22]</a></sup></blockquote> Especially resonating with TI’s, and fueling their paranoia, is that:<br /> <blockquote class=”gmail-letter”> Under the title “Online Covert Action”, the document details a variety of means to engage in “influence and info ops” as well as “disruption and computer net attack,” while dissecting how human beings can be manipulated using “leaders,” “trust,” “obedience” and “compliance”… The documents lay out theories of how humans interact with one another, particularly online, and then attempt to identify ways to influence the outcomes—or “game” it…<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-JTRIG_25-1”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-JTRIG-25”>[22]</a></sup></blockquote> This all “confirms” what “they” are doing to the poor TIs. JTRIG explains why they do not know whom to trust even among themselves, because, you see, “many” TI web sites and individuals are actually disinformation peddlers planted by “them”:<br /> <blockquote class=”gmail-letter”> Anyone who has spent any time searching online for information about the kind of domestic counterintelligence operations (and vigilante operations by corrupt cops and former cops) described in this website, has seen a lot of disinformation – even if it was not recognized as such. The vast majority of websites purporting to be efforts to expose “organized stalking,” “gang stalking,” “targeted individuals,” etc., are in fact, government websites intended to give the impression that all claims about such stalking are delusional.<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-26”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-26”>[23]</a></sup></blockquote> As a result of this intense interest in JTRIG, TIs began to deeply infest Greenwald’s comments section, certain they had found a receptive home. Typical of their prodigious ranting were such gems as:<br /> <blockquote class=”gmail-letter”> The torturers have pumped my legs and arms so full of nanodevices where the legs and the feet have now become grossly bloated. They then remotely mobilize the devices to simulate large crawling insects. Excite nerve endings, at will. The right eye, the entire left face, entire left side of head, left eyebrow, all eject clouds of high velocity, highly vibrational nanocrystal fibres into the air from deep within. The pain and discomfort are unspeakable. Nanodevices are vibrating in cervical lymph nodes at will. And nerve pain endings are excited all night.</blockquote> Eventually, all of these tragic, pitiable people had to be banned<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-27”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-27”>[Note 4]</a></sup>&nbsp;because they were taking over the discussions in nearly every NSA related article. This, of course, simply convinced them that Snowden,&nbsp;<em>and</em>&nbsp;his chosen journalist, Greenwald, are both “false flags” actually operating for “them”.<br /> <h2> <span class=”gmail-mw-headline” id=”gmail-Are_they_all_lunatics.3F”>Are they all lunatics?</span><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection”><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection-bracket”>[</span><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/w/index.php?title=Targeted_Individuals&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5” title=”Edit section: Are they all lunatics?”>edit</a><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection-bracket”>]</span></span></h2> <div class=”gmail-thumb gmail-tright”> <div class=”gmail-thumbinner”> <a class=”gmail-image” href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/File:Bloodshot_eye.jpg”><img alt=”” class=”gmail-thumbimage” height=”225” src=”reqs/upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Bloodshot_eye.jpg/300px-Bloodshot_eye.jpg” width=”300” /></a> <br /> <div class=”gmail-thumbcaption”> <div class=”gmail-magnify”> </div> If these grave and mysterious symptoms appear, cease taking all medication and start reading&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/David_Icke” title=”David Icke”>David Icke</a>’s books!</div> </div> </div> Not necessarily all TIs—though probably many—clearly suffer from mental illness in a clinical sense. A former national security reporter for the&nbsp;<em>Washington Post</em>, Sharon Weinberger, has provided in-depth coverage of the TI phenomenon.<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-28”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-28”>[24]</a></sup>&nbsp;As she noted in an interview about her work:<br /> <blockquote class=”gmail-letter”> Human experience is not clear-cut, and phantom pains, voices, and feelings of being watched or followed are all a part of this experience. Many, many people will experience fleeting auditory hallucinations in their lives. Who hasn’t had the feeling of “being watched?” <br /> I think that what we are seeing is a continuum of human experience that ranges from the common to uncommon: Common might be: “I think my neighbor is watching me”; to what some regard as kooky but not psychotic: “I was kidnapped by aliens”; and finally to what many regard as psychotic (“The government is controlling my mind”)<br /> Maybe we shouldn’t be so quick to judge what’s “psychotic.” I do think dismissing everyone who believes in mind control as schizophrenic is a mistake-not because I believe they are victims of mind control-but because I feel that’s too simplistic.<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-29”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-29”>[25]</a></sup></blockquote> Weinberger points out that not all TI’s report the more extreme symptoms, and auditory hallucinations may have neurological causes that are not yet well understood. It can be hard to know where eccentricity ends and clinical mental illness begins. The voices, the sense of being watched, of being physically molested, have been reported throughout human history and ascribed to the causative agents popularly feared at the time, e.g., demons, aliens, and now government weapons and surveillance. Perhaps many TIs are trying to make sense of genuine experiences in the terms their culture makes available to them.<br /> ome TIs are successful professionals, and many have decent marriages and other relationships. The renowned African-American writer Gloria Naylor<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-30”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-30”>[Note 5]</a></sup>&nbsp;published a memoir in 2005 setting forth what she describes as being targeted by the U.S. government for surveillance, harassment and “mind control.”<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-31”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-31”>[26]</a></sup>&nbsp;She did see a psychiatrist and consider that she could be having psychotic episodes, but anti-psychotic medication did not stop the voices or the sense that she was being watched and stalked.<br /> Certainly TI symptoms can do serious damage to people’s lives. Weinberger interviewed a young medical doctor, anesthesiologist Ed Moore, who discontinued practicing medicine, and his initially supportive wife eventually filed for divorce. Moore was hospitalized with depression and auditory hallucinations, but no treatment—including medication—alleviated his sensation of being harassed with “electronic voices.” He eventually took comfort in the support he believes he found at online TI message boards, but states he is skeptical of “wacky claims” from some of his fellow targets.<br /> <h3> <span class=”gmail-mw-headline” id=”gmail-Views_of_mental_health_professionals”>Views of mental health professionals</span><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection”><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection-bracket”>[</span><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/w/index.php?title=Targeted_Individuals&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6” title=”Edit section: Views of mental health professionals”>edit</a><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection-bracket”>]</span></span></h3> Already in 2008, psychologists and psychiatrists were concerned about the burgeoning TI phenomenon. The Internet’s midwifing TIs into communities was something new in the field and needed examination.<br /> <blockquote class=”gmail-letter”> Dr. Ralph Hoffman, a psychiatry professor at Yale who studies delusions, said a growing number of his research subjects have told him of visiting mind-control sites, and finding in them confirmation of their own experiences. “The views of these belief systems are like a shark that has to be constantly fed,” Dr. Hoffman said. “If you don’t feed the delusion, sooner or later it will die out or diminish on its own accord. The key thing is that it needs to be repetitively reinforced.” That is what the Web sites do, he said.<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-32”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-32”>[27]</a></sup></blockquote> The problem that presents, though, is that when enough people share a delusion, medical science has said it ceases to be one. Psychologist Vaughan Bell has researched the effect of the Internet on mental illness and has concluded that TI sites are “likely psychotic.” However:<br /> <blockquote class=”gmail-letter”> The extent of the community, Dr. Bell said, poses a paradox to the traditional way delusion is defined under the diagnostic guidelines of the American Psychiatric Association, which says that if a belief is held by a person’s “culture or subculture,” it is not a delusion.</blockquote> But even if the TI sites&nbsp;<em>are</em>&nbsp;psychotic, is that so bad? Bell isn’t sure. “Things like social support, all of these positive social aspects are very good for people’s mental illness,” he said. “I wouldn’t say it’s entirely and completely positive, but it can be positive.” Dr. Ken Duckworth, the medical director for the National Alliance on Mental Illness, observes: “This is a very complex little corner. Some people may find it’s healing, but these are really hard questions. The Internet isn’t a cause of mental illness, it’s a complicating new variable.”<br /> <h3> <span class=”gmail-mw-headline” id=”gmail-Myron_May.2C_Targeted_Individual”>Myron May, Targeted Individual</span><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection”><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection-bracket”>[</span><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/w/index.php?title=Targeted_Individuals&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7” title=”Edit section: Myron May, Targeted Individual”>edit</a><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection-bracket”>]</span></span></h3> Little doubt exists that Myron May was mentally ill before he was shot dead by Florida police in November of 2014. In the course of a gun-toting rampage at the Florida State University library, May shot and wounded three before law enforcement ended both him and his shooting spree (an occasion where law enforcement’s shooting an African-American male wasn’t especially controversial).<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-33”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-33”>[28]</a></sup><br /> May had belonged to a Facebook group called “Targeted Individuals International.” A week before he gunned down people at FSU May had left a voicemail for one of his fellow TIs, claiming, “I am currently being cooked in my chair. I devised a scheme where I was going to expose this once and for all and I really need you.” He added: “I do not want to die in vain.” An hour before the shooting he sent an email to this same TI, stating, “I’ve been getting hit with the direct energy weapon in my chest all evening. It hurts really bad right now.”<br /> Formerly a high-powered employment lawyer in Texas, May left a lucrative career representing management for a smaller firm on the side of labor—because he didn’t want to help corporations.<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-34”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-34”>[29]</a></sup>&nbsp;Then he tried his hand at criminal defense as a public defender in New Mexico. A month before his shooting rampage, May had been a successful and respected associate trial attorney in the felony division of the Third Judicial District Attorney’s Office in Las Cruces, NM.<br /> May’s former girlfriend from New Mexico—Danielle Nixon, a physician—said he’d recently had a mental health evaluation and she’d been concerned about his increasingly erratic behavior and eventually would only meet him in public places. Nixon said May had seen a therapist who was not alarmed: “My honest feeling is because Myron was a lawyer and he was high functioning, people overestimated him. They didn’t think he was as sick as he was.” In September of 2014, May checked himself into a mental health unit which released him only four days later.<br /> Nixon continued to worry about May after breaking up with him, and when he showed up at her apartment she called police who reported: “Myron has recently developed a severe mental disorder. Myron believes that the police are after him and are bugging his phone and car, as well as placing cameras in his home and car.” Additionally, May was sending packages to friends to “warn” them of the attackers who were after him. In early October 2014, May resigned from the prosecutor’s office, to the surprise of his co-workers.<br /> Later in October May made his way to Florida and a month later committed the FSU shooting which ended his own torment—with the “help” of local cops. Many TIs, however, regard May as a martyr, one who was “murdered, forced to defend the world from our tyrannical government.”<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-35”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-35”>[30]</a></sup><br /> <h2> <span class=”gmail-mw-headline” id=”gmail-The_only_actual_.22targeting.22_going_on”>The only&nbsp;<em>actual</em>&nbsp;“targeting” going on</span><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection”><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection-bracket”>[</span><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/w/index.php?title=Targeted_Individuals&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8” title=’Edit section: The only actual “targeting” going on’>edit</a><span class=”gmail-mw-editsection-bracket”>]</span></span></h2> <table class=”gmail-cquote”> <tbody> <tr> <td><div> “”For those suffering from psychotronic attacks, you need a defense system. Defend yourself from remote EEG by covering your head with an aluminum beanie. Make sure to wear a cotton cap below (I use the lightweight chemotherapy caps).&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Not_even_wrong” title=”Not even wrong”>The aluminum foil beanie should cover the frontal, temporal and parietal lobe, as you want to cover your speech and auditory areas of the brain</a>. To defend yourself from heart rate monitoring, hang a personal Quwave defender from your neck. Recommend buying a couple of safety vests and coating the insides with 6 layers of aluminum foil (the reflective sides out). Then sow the safety vests together, against each other.</div> </td> </tr> <tr> <td><cite>—<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Poe%27s_Law” title=”Poe’s Law”>Instructions on usage</a>&nbsp;from someone who actually bought the QuWave Defender<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-36”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-36”>[31]</a></sup></cite></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> The population identifying as “Targeted Individuals”&nbsp;<em>is</em>&nbsp;actually being targeted—not by evil government or&nbsp;<a class=”gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Reptilian” title=”Reptilian”>other</a>&nbsp;forces—but by enterprising hucksters and scam artists who exploit the fear and ignorance of these often unstable unfortunates.<br /> There are various products purporting to protect TI’s from remote mind control invasion, for example, the “QuWave Defender.” For a mere $297, TIs can acquire a “personal defender” unit that will supposedly protect them from “<a class=”gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Vague” title=”Vague”>Electronic harassment, mind control, V2K, psychic or HAARP</a>”. Or, if they’re willing to dip into the kids’ tuition fund, TIs can obtain a “powerful briefcase defender” for the bargain price of $1150.<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-37”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-37”>[32]</a></sup>&nbsp;This amazing product has been sold on Amazon,<sup class=”gmail-reference” id=”gmail-cite_ref-38”><a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Targeted_Individuals#cite_note-38”>[33]</a></sup>&nbsp;with an accompanying product description loaded with enough crank buzzwords to fill several pseudoscience bingo cards:<br /> <blockquote class=”gmail-letter”> Protection for Targeted Individuals from Electronic Harassment and Psychotronic Attacks caused by ELF, HAARP, Implants, Microwaves, Psychic Attacks etc. [The QuWave Defender] produces a&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Scalar_wave” title=”Scalar wave”>Scalar Field</a>&nbsp;that&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Pseudoscience” title=”Pseudoscience”>interferes with external and internal negative harmful signals</a>, and uses&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Solfeggio_frequencies” title=”Solfeggio frequencies”>Solfeggio Waves</a>&nbsp;to convert the electronic and&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Psychic” title=”Psychic”>psychic</a>&nbsp;attacks to&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Woo” title=”Woo”>positive energy and strengthen the human bio-field</a>…. <br /> We have combined our Scalar Wave Technology with Solfeggio Frequencies and developed&nbsp;<a class=”gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Crankery” title=”Crankery”>a device which constantly beams the waves directly into your brain</a>&nbsp;via a Scalar Bio-Field. The Defender has&nbsp;<a href=”http://rationalwiki.org/wiki/Placebo_effect” title=”Placebo effect”>helped many targeted individuals cope with their harassment to be able to live a happier life.</a></blockquote> QuWave.com is only one of many scammers looking to make a fast buck from TI’s. I’m sick of it by now; I want you to see that truth and love are scarce; and that’s something that we have to change; or there won’t be any world here at all.</div> <div> <br /></div> <div> The point is there are really great things in store for everyone, benefits that even the richest people on this place will see and be happy about–and really understand that they too were being tortured by the lies keeping us from evolving to fully utilize the possibilities and benefits of our true existence, of virtual reality.&nbsp; It’s like night and day, and to sit here and have to argue with you about how important it is that we act quickly to “end world hunger” while I’m promising nothing to you but&nbsp;<i>near immortality for doing it;&nbsp;</i>I mean, I think you look really stupid.&nbsp;&nbsp;</div> <div> <br /></div> <div> It really does appear to me that you are waiting for “better promises” or “bigger things” to fall out of the sky as we wander in the desert; and I am here to tell you that it’s salt.&nbsp;&nbsp;<b>Manna</b>&nbsp;from Heaven, is&nbsp;<a href=”http://prometheus.reallyhim.com/ ” target=”_blank”>bath salt</a>, flying down from the sky into my hands, holy sacrament…&nbsp;<i>for the&nbsp;<a href=”./2017/09/duck-duck-golden-egg.html” target=”_blank”>m</a>&nbsp;<a href=”./2017/08/the-color-of-understanding.html” target=”_blank”>an</a>.&nbsp;&nbsp;</i>Listen, this is&nbsp;<b>how</b>&nbsp;<a href=”./WHO.html” target=”_blank”>Jesus Christ</a>&nbsp;<a href=”http://erichow.reallyhjim.com/ ” target=”_blank”>ends addiction</a>, and&nbsp;<a href=”./2017/07/lets-go-skinny-dipping-come-on-itll-be_6.html” target=”_blank”>your apparent aversion</a>&nbsp;to “good feeling good.”</div> </div> </center> </div> <span </div> </div> <div class=”gmail_quote”> <div dir=”ltr”> <div> <strong><br /></strong> <strong>rm</strong>&nbsp;(short for&nbsp;<em>remove</em>) is a basic&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/UNIX_command” target=”_blank” title=”UNIX command”>UNIX command</a>&nbsp;used to remove objects such as files, directories,&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Device_node” target=”_blank” title=”Device node”>device nodes</a>,&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Symbolic_link” target=”_blank” title=”Symbolic link”>symbolic links</a>, and so on from the filesystem. To be more precise,&nbsp;<strong>rm</strong>&nbsp;removes references to objects from the filesystem, where those objects might have had multiple references (for example, a file with two different names), and the objects themselves are discarded only when all references have been removed and no programs still have open handles to the objects.<br /> <br /></div> <div> This allows for scenarios where a program can open a file, immediately remove it from the filesystem, and then use it for temporary space, knowing that the file’s space will be reclaimed after the program exits, even if it exits by crashing.<br /> <br /></div> <div> <strong>rm</strong>&nbsp;generally does not destroy file data, since its purpose is really merely to unlink references, and the filesystem space freed may still contain leftover data from the removed file. This can be a security concern in some cases, and hardened versions sometimes provide for wiping out the data as the last link is being cut, and programs such as&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shred_(Unix)” target=”_blank” title=”Shred (Unix)”>shred</a>&nbsp;are available which specifically provide data wiping capability.</div> <div class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-separator” style=”text-align: center;”> <a href=”http://chuck-nbc.fandom.com/wiki/The_Intersect” target=”_blank”><img border=”0” height=”130” src=”reqs/4.bp.blogspot.com/-R_GlJ3ZIJ0Y/WeJo_96K9vI/AAAAAAAAJMc/dtlauXpxyB0TsIECf4_CNVHZNQekgqkSACLcBGAs/s400/Screenshot+2017-10-14+at+10.55.17+AM.png” width=”400” /></a><br /> <br /></div> <div> <strong>Isaac Asimov</strong>&nbsp;(<span class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-nowrap”><span class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-IPA m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-nopopups m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-noexcerpt”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA/English” target=”_blank” title=”Help:IPA/English”>/<span title=”/ˈ/: primary stress follows”>ˈ</span><span title=”/æ/: ‘a’ in ‘bad’”>æ</span><span title=“‘z’ in ‘zoom’”>z</span><span title=”/ɪ/: ‘i’ in ‘kit’”>ɪ</span><span title=“‘m’ in ‘my’”>m</span><span title=”/ɒ/: ‘o’ in ‘body’”>ɒ</span><span title=“‘v’ in ‘vie’”>v</span>/</a></span></span>;<sup class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-reference” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-cite_ref-2”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Asimov#cite_note-2” target=”_blank”>[2]</a></sup>&nbsp;born&nbsp;<strong>Isa<wbr></wbr>ak Ozimov</strong>;&nbsp;<abbr title=”circa”>c.</abbr>&nbsp;January 2, 1920<sup class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-reference” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-cite_ref-birthday_1-1”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Asimov#cite_note-birthday-1” target=”_blank”>[1]</a></sup>&nbsp;– April 6, 1992) was a&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jewish_Americans” target=”_blank” title=”Jewish Americans”>Jewish-American</a>&nbsp;writer and professor of&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biochemistry” target=”_blank” title=”Biochemistry”>biochemistry</a>&nbsp;at&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boston_University” target=”_blank” title=”Boston University”>Boston University</a>. He was known for his works of&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Science_fiction” target=”_blank” title=”Science fiction”>science fiction</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Popular_science” target=”_blank” title=”Popular science”>popular science</a>. Asimov was a&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_prolific_writers” target=”_blank” title=”List of prolific writers”>prolific writer</a>, and wrote or edited more than 500 books and an estimated 90,000 letters and&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Postcard” target=”_blank” title=”Postcard”>postcards</a>.<sup class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-reference” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-cite_ref-3”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Asimov#cite_note-3” target=”_blank”>[3]</a></sup>&nbsp;His books have been published in 9 of the 10 major categories of the&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dewey_Decimal_Classification” target=”_blank” title=”Dewey Decimal Classification”>Dewey Decimal Classification</a>.<sup class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-reference” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-cite_ref-AsimovFAQ-DeweyDecimal_4-0”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Asimov#cite_note-AsimovFAQ-DeweyDecimal-4” target=”_blank”>[4]</a></sup><br /> <br /></div> <div> Asimov wrote&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hard_science_fiction” target=”_blank” title=”Hard science fiction”>hard science fiction</a>&nbsp;and, along with&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_A._Heinlein” target=”_blank” title=”Robert A. Heinlein”>Robert A. Heinlein</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arthur_C._Clarke” target=”_blank” title=”Arthur C. Clarke”>Arthur C. Clarke</a>, he was considered one of the “Big Three” science fiction writers during his lifetime.<sup class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-reference” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-cite_ref-5”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Asimov#cite_note-5” target=”_blank”>[5]</a></sup>&nbsp;Asimov’s most famous work is the&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Foundation_series” target=”_blank” title=”Foundation series”><em>Foundation</em>&nbsp;Series</a>;<sup class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-reference” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-cite_ref-6”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Asimov#cite_note-6” target=”_blank”>[6]</a></sup>&nbsp;his other major series are the&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Asimov%27s_Galactic_Empire_Series” target=”_blank” title=”Isaac Asimov’s Galactic Empire Series”><em>Galactic Empire</em>&nbsp;series</a>&nbsp;and the&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Asimov%27s_Robot_Series” target=”_blank” title=”Isaac Asimov’s Robot Series”><em>Robot</em>&nbsp;series</a>. The&nbsp;<em>Galactic Empire</em>&nbsp;novels are explicitly set in earlier history of the same fictional universe as the&nbsp;<em>Foundation</em>&nbsp;series. Later, beginning with&nbsp;<em><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Foundation%27s_Edge” target=”_blank” title=”Foundation’s Edge”>Foundation’s Edge</a></em>, he linked this distant future to the Robot and Spacer stories, creating a unified “<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Future_history” target=”_blank” title=”Future history”>future history</a>” for his stories much like those pioneered by Robert A. Heinlein and previously produced by&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cordwainer_Smith” target=”_blank” title=”Cordwainer Smith”>Cordwainer Smith</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Poul_Anderson” target=”_blank” title=”Poul Anderson”>Poul Anderson</a>.<sup class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-reference” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-cite_ref-7”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Asimov#cite_note-7” target=”_blank”>[7]</a></sup>&nbsp;He wrote hundreds of short stories, including the&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Social_science_fiction” target=”_blank” title=”Social science fiction”>social science fiction</a>&nbsp;novelette “<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nightfall_(Asimov_novelette_and_novel)” target=”_blank” title=”Nightfall (Asimov novelette and novel)”>Nightfall</a>”, which in 1964 was voted by the&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Science_Fiction_Writers_of_America” target=”_blank” title=”Science Fiction Writers of America”>Science Fiction Writers of America</a>&nbsp;the best short science fiction story of all time. Asimov wrote the&nbsp;<em><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lucky_Starr_series” target=”_blank” title=”Lucky Starr series”>Lucky Starr</a></em><br /> <br /></div> <div> According to the biblical&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Genesis” target=”_blank” title=”Book of Genesis”>Book of Genesis</a>,&nbsp;<strong>Isaac</strong>&nbsp;(<span class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-nowrap”><span class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-IPA m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-nopopups m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-noexcerpt”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA/English” target=”_blank” title=”Help:IPA/English”>/<span title=”/ˈ/: primary stress follows”>ˈ</span><span title=”/aɪ/: ‘i’ in ‘tide’”>aɪ</span><span title=“‘z’ in ‘zoom’”>z</span><span title=”/ə/: ‘a’ in ‘about’”>ə</span><span title=“‘k’ in ‘kind’”>k</span>/</a></span></span>;&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language” target=”_blank” title=”Hebrew language”>Hebr<wbr></wbr>ew</a>:&nbsp;<span dir=”rtl” lang=”he”>יִצְחָק</span>,&nbsp;<small><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Modern_Hebrew” target=”_blank” title=”Modern Hebrew”>Modern</a></small>&nbsp;<em>Yiṣḥáq</em>,&nbsp;<small><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tiberian_vocalization” target=”_blank” title=”Tiberian vocalization”>Ti<wbr></wbr>berian</a></small>&nbsp;<em>Yiṣḥāq</em>;&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-mw-redirect” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic_language” target=”_blank” title=”Arabic language”>Arabic</a>:&nbsp;<span dir=”rtl” lang=”ar”>إسحٰق/إ<wbr></wbr>سحاق</span>‎‎,&nbsp;<span class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-Unicode” title=”DIN 31635 Arabic”><em>Isḥāq</em></span>) was the son of&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abraham” target=”_blank” title=”Abraham”>Abraham</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sarah” target=”_blank” title=”Sarah”>Sarah</a>&nbsp;and father of&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jacob” target=”_blank” title=”Jacob”>Jacob</a>; his name means “he will laugh”, reflecting Sarah’s response when told that she would have a child.<sup class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-reference” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-cite_ref-FOOTNOTEdeClaise-Walford2000647_1-0”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac#cite_note-FOOTNOTEdeClaise-Walford2000647-1” target=”_blank”>[1]</a></sup>&nbsp;He was one of the three&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Patriarchs_(Bible)” target=”_blank” title=”Patriarchs (Bible)”>patriarchs</a>&nbsp;of the&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Israelites” target=”_blank” title=”Israelites”>Israelites</a>, the only one whose name was not changed, and the only one who did not move out of&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canaan” target=”_blank” title=”Canaan”>Canaan</a>.<sup class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-reference” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-cite_ref-FOOTNOTEdeClaise-Walford2000647_1-1”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac#cite_note-FOOTNOTEdeClaise-Walford2000647-1” target=”_blank”>[1]</a></sup>&nbsp;He died when he was 180&nbsp;years old, the longest-lived of the three.<sup class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-reference” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-cite_ref-FOOTNOTEdeClaise-Walford2000647_1-2”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac#cite_note-FOOTNOTEdeClaise-Walford2000647-1” target=”_blank”>[1]</a></sup><br /> <br /></div> <div> In the&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-new” href=”http://riffwiki.com/index.php?title=X86_assembly_language&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1” target=”_blank” title=”X86 assembly language (page does not exist)”>x86 assembly language</a>, the&nbsp;<strong>MOV</strong>&nbsp;instruction is a&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-new” href=”http://riffwiki.com/index.php?title=Mnemonic&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1” target=”_blank” title=”Mnemonic (page does not exist)”>mnemonic</a>&nbsp;for the copying of data from one location to another. The x86 assembly language has a number of different move instructions. Depending on whether the program is in a 16-bit or 32-bit code segment (in&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-new” href=”http://riffwiki.com/index.php?title=Protected_mode&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1” target=”_blank” title=”Protected mode (page does not exist)”>protected mode</a>) and whether an override instruction prefix is used, a MOV instruction may transfer&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-new” href=”http://riffwiki.com/index.php?title=8-bit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1” target=”_blank” title=”8-bit (page does not exist)”>8-bits</a>,&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-new” href=”http://riffwiki.com/index.php?title=16-bit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1” target=”_blank” title=”16-bit (page does not exist)”>16-bits</a>, or&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-new” href=”http://riffwiki.com/index.php?title=32-bit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1” target=”_blank” title=”32-bit (page does not exist)”>32-bits</a>&nbsp;of data (or&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-new” href=”http://riffwiki.com/index.php?title=64-bit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1” target=”_blank” title=”64-bit (page does not exist)”>64-bits</a>&nbsp;in x86-64 mode). Data may be copied to and from memory and registers.<sup class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-reference” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-cite_ref-1”><a href=”http://riffwiki.com/MOV_(x86_instruction)#cite_note-1” target=”_blank”>[1]</a></sup><br /> <br /></div> <div> The word move for this operation is a misnomer: it has little to do with the physical concept of moving an object from A to B, with place A then becoming empty; a MOV instead makes a&nbsp;<em>copy</em>&nbsp;of the&nbsp;<em>state</em>&nbsp;of the object at A and overwrites the old state of B in this process. This is reflected in some other assembly languages by using words like&nbsp;<em>load</em>,&nbsp;<em>store</em>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<em>copy</em>&nbsp;inste<wbr></wbr>ad of&nbsp;<em>move</em>.</div> <div> <address> <div class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-comment-meta m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-comment-meta-data”> <span class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-comment-author m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-vcard” style=”color: rgb(0 , 0 , 0);”>h0mer</span>&nbsp;<span class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-published”><abbr class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-comment-date” title=”Thursday, December 8th, 2016, 7:42 pm”>December 8, 2016</abbr>&nbsp;at&nbsp;<abbr class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-comment-time” title=”Thursday, December 8th, 2016, 7:42 pm”>7:42 pm</abbr></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-permalink” href=”http://www.digital5k.com/aol-progz-a-digital-throw-back-to-aol-1995/#comment-4279” target=”_blank” title=”Permalink to comment 4279”>Permalink</a>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-comment-reply-link” href=”http://www.digital5k.com/aol-progz-a-digital-throw-back-to-aol-1995/?replytocom=4279#respond” rel=”nofollow” target=”_blank”>Reply</a></div> <div class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-comment-text”> <div> I miss those days man. I remember getting my first copy of VB 3.0 from a mass mail in the chatroom. (I remember being so intrigued by Pepsi, Soylent Green Server/MMer, FiRe Toolz, AOHell, etc.) Once I got my hands on VB 3.0 I began programming like a son of a bitch (Yeah I was like 11 years old lol) From laggers, to punters, chat commands, phishers, email bombers, ascii shops, macro builders, etc. I remember losing my AOL account for a.) scrolling a middle finger in the Nickelodeon chatroom followed by me email bombing some dude with over 2,0000 emails. (Yeah my dad was pissed, he forbid me from logging on and told me was lost our AOL subscription. Little did he know I ran a key logger on the computer and found out his login info.)</div> <div> Oh man, do I miss the good ole days of AOL progz lol good times.</div> </div> <ol 1995.</span></div> <div class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-hentry m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-post m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-publish m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-post_tag-progs” id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-post-18”> <h1 class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-post-title m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859entry-title”> <a href=”http://www.digital5k.com/aol-progz-a-digital-throw-back-to-aol-1995/” target=”_blank”>aol progz… a digital throw back to AOL, 1995.</a></h1> <div class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-byline”> By&nbsp;<span class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-author m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-vcard”><a class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-url m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-fn m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-n” href=”http://www.digital5k.com/author/digital/” rel=”author” target=”_blank” title=”digital”>digital</a></span>&nbsp;on&nbsp;<abbr class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-published” title=”Tuesday, July 2nd, 2013, 6:55 pm”>July 2, 2013</abbr></div> <div class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859entry-content”> <div> one of the main reasons that i decided to recreate my&nbsp;<a href=”http://www.digital5k.com/” target=”_blank”>digital5k.com</a>&nbsp;website was the constant memories of the AOL progz days.&nbsp; i won’t lie, there are redundant reminders of my AOL/visual basic (vb)/C++ childhood.&nbsp; it was a great time in life and the internet, if you ask me.&nbsp; let’s start off by how it all caught my attention and obsession… ascii art – which doomed my future and solidified my career in computers, programming, development and marketing.</div> <div id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-maincontent”> <div id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-outputFigDisplay”> <pre id=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-taag_output_text”> .___.__ .__ __ .__ .__________ __| _/|__| ____ |__|/ |______ | | | ____/ | __ / __ | | |/ ___\| \ __\__ \ | | |____ \| |/ / / /_/ | | / /_/ &gt; || | / __ | |__/ \ &lt; \____ | |__\___ /|__||__| (____ /____/______ /__|_ / /_____/ / / /</pre> </div> </div> <div> yep, ascii art was the one little element that attack my attention span and made me say ‘whoa, that’s pretty cool’.&nbsp; better known in those days as scrollers or macros.&nbsp; a macro is simple font characters put together to form a type of pre-digital art.&nbsp; i’ll never forget the first time i signed into AOL and say that beautiful scroll ascii art by ao-hell.<br /> <br /></div> <div> <div style=”text-align: center;”> <a href=”http://www.digital5k.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/AOHellSplashScreen.jpg” target=”_blank”><img alt=”AOHellSplashScreen” class=”m_-6126058758198551859m_6231623775613442859gmail-aligncenter” height=”212” src=”reqs/images-blogger-opensocial.googleusercontent.com/gadgets/proxy?url=http%253A%252F%252Fwww.digital5k.com%252Fwp-content%252Fuploads%252F2013%252F07%252FAOHellSplashScreen.jpg&amp;container=blogger&amp;gadget=a&amp;rewriteMime=image%252F*” width=”361” /></a><br /> <br /></div> </div> <div> i was in 6th grade.&nbsp; who knows how old i was, i don’t feel like doing the math.&nbsp; i had just moved to the hell hole known as _____ from Houston, Texas.&nbsp; i had no friends.&nbsp; i knew nobody.&nbsp; i just wanted to go home.&nbsp; since Texas schools let out a few weeks earlier, i had some time to kill.&nbsp; a very dangerous thing for a teenager.&nbsp; what is a borderline anti social teen to do in a city with no friends?&nbsp; go on the internet with the elite speed of&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/56_kbit/s_modem” rel=”noopener noreferrer” target=”_blank”><strong>56 bits per second</strong></a>.<br /> <br /></div> <div> </div> <div> for those of us who remember, AOL was very… fucked.&nbsp; the horrible chatrooms, stupid interface, laggy system and overall confusing nature, yet – it’s all we had.&nbsp; the internet was a different place back in 1995.&nbsp; images of a woman’s breasts were downloaded one pixel line at a time.&nbsp; often stopping right above the nipple or right below the belly button.&nbsp; there were no scams, very little spam, limited advertising and an innocence that can never be restored.&nbsp; the internet was the preacher’s virgin daughter that was just getting ready to leave home, go off to college and get fucked, hard.<br /> <br /></div> <div> it took 3-4 attempts to connect to AOL back then, i would go on to later know the swift backdoor, alternate numbers and general brute force attacks that would prioritize my place in dial up line.&nbsp; once you gained a stable connection, it was a release of endorphins that no drug has been able to reignite in my brain.&nbsp; it was instant freedom.&nbsp; no reality, no physical or gravitational limits, nobody to answer to.&nbsp; it was an open digital playground with visual basic as monkey bars and the rush of adrenaline for swings.&nbsp; it was a
